The RES-SEARCH query of the Sihot WEB interface is ignoring the CENTRAL-GUEST-ID filter. All returned records are within the given date range and having the value zero in the returned CENTRAL-GUEST-ID xml element.

The following example is passing into the CENTRAL-GUEST-ID filter xml element the GID field value (109074) from a Room-move (Sihot operation code RM) notification (sent by Sihot XML interface to our AcuServer) happened on the 17th of May from A103 to A117 for the client Pedro Sol√© Barrio (PCIID==213183, AN==490301, DEP=22-05-2017) - we can not use the Account number (AN xml element) because it is sometimes zero and it is like the PCIID element not supported by the WEB interface:

17.05.2017 17:14:22,757 INFO  - <?xml version="1.0" encoding="cp1252"?>

</SIHOT-Document>
